17 3 17 AMAZON LG A939KBGS 4 2022-08-21 Kim I like it I like it . I’ll start by saying, I’d never have bought myself this vacuum as it is pretty cost prohibitive . My mother bought it for me as a gift and I’ve been pleasantly surprised . It has better suction than I expected it would . And since it is lightweight, I grab it almost everyday instead of a broom for my tile floors and instead of my bulky vacuum for carpets .By far, the most valuable feature is the fact that u don’t have to open that canister to empty it out . I’ve had other stick vacuums in the past that, while emptying it, I usually felt that I was just spreading all the contents around again . When u dock this vacuum, all the contents r sucked into an internal bag . My FAVORITE feature .I have 2 greyhounds that seem to continuously shed fur . So the ability to grab this vacuum rather push the fur around with a broom is much better .I’ve never tried the mop feature as it seems sort of pointless to me…which is maybe why this thing is priced so high .Like I said, I would never pay $1000 for a vacuum… but I LOVE the self-emptying feature… and it’s suction power will surprise! like start saying never bought vacuum pretty cost prohibitive 48 6 48 AMAZON LG A939KBGS 5 2022-07-24 Terry J. Keaton Expensive but with value - little update Expensive but with value - little update . We have gone through all kinds of vacuums, corded, cordless, and robot . Still have a corded Dyson for deep, heavy cleaning . Went through the latest Dyson V11, nice machine but connections on the stick were weak, started breaking . Went to the new Shark, nice but loud . Worked well, a bit heavy . Saw a commercial for this LG and checked it out . After all their TV and oven we have are exceptional . Turns out the vacuum is pretty nifty too . Yeah, expensive, but the technology and abilities make it worth it . It has two batteries, so use time is extended a long time . It is very lightweight, surprisingly so . The suction is strong, no problem picking up bird seed, popcorn, and other normal carpet detritus . No switch to push between carpet and flooring . The fringe on the carpet has not (yet) gotten caught up, even after pushing it up more than halfway . That actually straightens out the fringe . Easy to lift over because of the lack of weight . So far haven’t needed to use the compact button, would take a lot of vacuuming to fill it up enough . Really nice to just stick it in the stand and have the dirt get automatically sucked out and into a bag . Simple to put together, just put on the non-skid tape, set the unit on the base, plug it in, attach accessories . Just wish there was some storage for the floor mops . Ended up velcroing the bag on the back of the stand . Also need a place to stick extra bags so I don’t forget where they are . Yep, really big complaints there . We believe this was well worth the cost .Little update concerning fringe . Purposely ran over the fringe numerous times from both sides . Was cringing, expecting screaming noise an stoppage from jamming . Nope, cringing unnecessarily, nothing happened . The fringe got sucked in, could see it kind of flapping on top of the brush, but no loud noise and no stopping or even slowing . We have gone through all kinds of vacuums, corded, cordless, and robot . Still have a corded Dyson for deep, heavy cleaning . Saw a commercial for this LG and checked it out . After all their TV and oven we have are exceptional . Turns out the vacuum is pretty nifty too . Yeah, expensive, but the technology and abilities make it worth it . It has two batteries, so use time is extended a long time . It is very lightweight, surprisingly so . The suction is strong, no problem picking up bird seed, popcorn, and other normal carpet detritus . No switch to push between carpet and flooring . The fringe on the carpet has not (yet) gotten caught up, even after pushing it up more than halfway . That actually straightens out the fringe . Easy to lift over because of the lack of weight . So far haven’t needed to use the compact button, would take a lot of vacuuming to fill it up enough . Really nice to just stick it in the stand and have the dirt get automatically sucked out and into a bag . Simple to put together, just put on the non-skid tape, set the unit on the base, plug it in, attach accessories . Just wish there was some storage for the floor mops . Ended up velcroing the bag on the back of the stand . Also need a place to stick extra bags so I don’t forget where they are . Yep, really big complaints there . Saw a commercial for this LG and checked it out . After all their TV and oven we have are exceptional . Turns out the vacuum is pretty nifty too . Yeah, expensive, but the technology and abilities make it worth it . It has two batteries, so use time is extended a long time . It is very lightweight, surprisingly so . The suction is strong, no problem picking up bird seed, popcorn, and other normal carpet detritus . No switch to push between carpet and flooring . The fringe on the carpet has not (yet) gotten caught up, even after pushing it up more than halfway . That actually straightens out the fringe . Easy to lift over because of the lack of weight . So far haven’t needed to use the compact button, would take a lot of vacuuming to fill it up enough . Really nice to just stick it in the stand and have the dirt get automatically sucked out and into a bag . Simple to put together, just put on the non-skid tape, set the unit on the base, plug it in, attach accessories . Just wish there was some storage for the floor mops . Ended up velcroing the bag on the back of the stand . Also need a place to stick extra bags so I don’t forget where they are . Yep, really big complaints there . We believe this was well worth the cost .Little update concerning fringe . Purposely ran over the fringe numerous times from both sides . Was cringing, expecting screaming noise an stoppage from jamming . Nope, cringing unnecessarily, nothing happened . The fringe got sucked in, could see it kind of flapping on top of the brush, but no loud noise and no stopping or even slowing . 64 6 64 AMAZON LG A939KBGS 5 2022-07-24 Terry J. Keaton Expensive but with value - little update Expensive but with value - little update . We have gone through all kinds of vacuums, corded, cordless, and robot . Still have a corded Dyson for deep, heavy cleaning . Went through the latest Dyson V11, nice machine but connections on the stick were weak, started breaking . Went to the new Shark, nice but loud . Worked well, a bit heavy . Saw a commercial for this LG and checked it out . After all their TV and oven we have are exceptional . Turns out the vacuum is pretty nifty too . Yeah, expensive, but the technology and abilities make it worth it . It has two batteries, so use time is extended a long time . It is very lightweight, surprisingly so . The suction is strong, no problem picking up bird seed, popcorn, and other normal carpet detritus . No switch to push between carpet and flooring . The fringe on the carpet has not (yet) gotten caught up, even after pushing it up more than halfway . That actually straightens out the fringe . Easy to lift over because of the lack of weight . So far haven’t needed to use the compact button, would take a lot of vacuuming to fill it up enough . Really nice to just stick it in the stand and have the dirt get automatically sucked out and into a bag . Simple to put together, just put on the non-skid tape, set the unit on the base, plug it in, attach accessories . Just wish there was some storage for the floor mops . Ended up velcroing the bag on the back of the stand . Also need a place to stick extra bags so I don’t forget where they are . Yep, really big complaints there . We believe this was well worth the cost .Little update concerning fringe . Purposely ran over the fringe numerous times from both sides . Was cringing, expecting screaming noise an stoppage from jamming . Nope, cringing unnecessarily, nothing happened . The fringe got sucked in, could see it kind of flapping on top of the brush, but no loud noise and no stopping or even slowing . 70 6 70 AMAZON LG A939KBGS 5 2022-07-24 Terry J. Keaton Expensive but with value - little update Expensive but with value - little update . We have gone through all kinds of vacuums, corded, cordless, and robot . Still have a corded Dyson for deep, heavy cleaning . Went through the latest Dyson V11, nice machine but connections on the stick were weak, started breaking . Went to the new Shark, nice but loud . Worked well, a bit heavy . Saw a commercial for this LG and checked it out . After all their TV and oven we have are exceptional . Turns out the vacuum is pretty nifty too . Yeah, expensive, but the technology and abilities make it worth it . It has two batteries, so use time is extended a long time . It is very lightweight, surprisingly so . The suction is strong, no problem picking up bird seed, popcorn, and other normal carpet detritus . No switch to push between carpet and flooring . The fringe on the carpet has not (yet) gotten caught up, even after pushing it up more than halfway . That actually straightens out the fringe . Easy to lift over because of the lack of weight . So far haven’t needed to use the compact button, would take a lot of vacuuming to fill it up enough . Really nice to just stick it in the stand and have the dirt get automatically sucked out and into a bag . Simple to put together, just put on the non-skid tape, set the unit on the base, plug it in, attach accessories . Just wish there was some storage for the floor mops . Ended up velcroing the bag on the back of the stand . Also need a place to stick extra bags so I don’t forget where they are . Yep, really big complaints there . We believe this was well worth the cost .Little update concerning fringe . Purposely ran over the fringe numerous times from both sides . Was cringing, expecting screaming noise an stoppage from jamming . Nope, cringing unnecessarily, nothing happened . The fringe got sucked in, could see it kind of flapping on top of the brush, but no loud noise and no stopping or even slowing . The fringe on the carpet has not (yet) gotten caught up, even after pushing it up more than halfway . That actually straightens out the fringe . Easy to lift over because of the lack of weight . So far haven’t needed to use the compact button, would take a lot of vacuuming to fill it up enough . Really nice to just stick it in the stand and have the dirt get automatically sucked out and into a bag . Simple to put together, just put on the non-skid tape, set the unit on the base, plug it in, attach accessories . Just wish there was some storage for the floor mops . Ended up velcroing the bag on the back of the stand . Also need a place to stick extra bags so I don’t forget where they are . Yep, really big complaints there . We believe this was well worth the cost .Little update concerning fringe . Purposely ran over the fringe numerous times from both sides . Was cringing, expecting screaming noise an stoppage from jamming . Nope, cringing unnecessarily, nothing happened . The fringe got sucked in, could see it kind of flapping on top of the brush, but no loud noise and no stopping or even slowing . We have gone through all kinds of vacuums, corded, cordless, and robot . Still have a corded Dyson for deep, heavy cleaning . Went through the latest Dyson V11, nice machine but connections on the stick were weak, started breaking . Went to the new Shark, nice but loud . Worked well, a bit heavy . Saw a commercial for this LG and checked it out . After all their TV and oven we have are exceptional . Turns out the vacuum is pretty nifty too . Yeah, expensive, but the technology and abilities make it worth it . It has two batteries, so use time is extended a long time . It is very lightweight, surprisingly so . The suction is strong, no problem picking up bird seed, popcorn, and other normal carpet detritus . No switch to push between carpet and flooring . The fringe on the carpet has not (yet) gotten caught up, even after pushing it up more than halfway . That actually straightens out the fringe . Easy to lift over because of the lack of weight . So far haven’t needed to use the compact button, would take a lot of vacuuming to fill it up enough . Really nice to just stick it in the stand and have the dirt get automatically sucked out and into a bag . Simple to put together, just put on the non-skid tape, set the unit on the base, plug it in, attach accessories . Just wish there was some storage for the floor mops . Ended up velcroing the bag on the back of the stand . Also need a place to stick extra bags so I don’t forget where they are . Yep, really big complaints there . We believe this was well worth the cost .Little update concerning fringe . Purposely ran over the fringe numerous times from both sides . Was cringing, expecting screaming noise an stoppage from jamming . Nope, cringing unnecessarily, nothing happened . The fringe got sucked in, could see it kind of flapping on top of the brush, but no loud noise and no stopping or even slowing . 89 8 89 AMAZON LG A939KBGS 3 2022-12-17 graywolf54 Great...but not with pets Great . . .but not with pets . This vacuum is really a very good product . It is light, does a good job on carpet and hard surfaces, and the auto-clean of the container is a nice feature . However, we have a Labrador retriever, and this product unfortunately continually clogs on her fur . Running the vacuum on max "turbo" helps reduce the clogging to a more manageable level - but you still have to periodically reach into the inlet and "hook" the fur out to unclog the device .The auto-clean feature also has trouble with pet fur . It either cannot remove it from the canister, or worse, it removes it from the canister but leaves it in the opening to the collection bag so it all falls on the floor when you remove the vacuum from the stand . We have even found the canister lid left open after the clean cycle because all the fur didn't get out - and the remaining contents all fell on the floor .We like the vacuum enough to keep experimenting with it - it's just somewhat disappointing that it handles pet fur so poorly . 97 8 97 AMAZON LG A939KBGS 3 2022-12-17 graywolf54 Great...but not with pets Great . . .but not with pets . This vacuum is really a very good product . It is light, does a good job on carpet and hard surfaces, and the auto-clean of the container is a nice feature . However, we have a Labrador retriever, and this product unfortunately continually clogs on her fur . Running the vacuum on max "turbo" helps reduce the clogging to a more manageable level - but you still have to periodically reach into the inlet and "hook" the fur out to unclog the device .The auto-clean feature also has trouble with pet fur . It either cannot remove it from the canister, or worse, it removes it from the canister but leaves it in the opening to the collection bag so it all falls on the floor when you remove the vacuum from the stand . We have even found the canister lid left open after the clean cycle because all the fur didn't get out - and the remaining contents all fell on the floor .We like the vacuum enough to keep experimenting with it - it's just somewhat disappointing that it handles pet fur so poorly .
